# Text Elements
Noon Sakinah ^sug8QNBC

Noon sakinah refers to Tanween and a Noon that has Sukoon ^tuZ18kZr

[[Clear Noon]] ^4Yur8chH

Clear noon or          is when you clearly 
pronounce the noon ^RrhhRCvk

This only happens if the letter before the noon is: ^U2srypll

For example: ^BUVayTzl

To easily know when you have a clear noon, check if there is a sukoon
on the noon, and if it is a tanween, then check for THESE signs: ^SOKPKLWN

This is NOT clear noon ^a92XunC2

THIS is clear noon  ^itWbzLrr

The Noon can have a Sukoon or not have a Sukoon ^P0BQCwGG

[[Merged Noon]] ^s8wVL6EE

A 'Merged Noon' happens when the noon is proceeded by: ^koKeD4Ba

If a noon is proceeded by one of the     letters then the 
pink letter will have a shaddah and the noon will be COMPLETELY
merged, meaning that you will not pronounced it AT ALL
For example: ^ntxZaYDU

Pink ^5VXEM0dO

A Merged Noon has two outcomes ^xkeBA94J

If a noon is proceeded by one of the        letters, then you will 
combine the noon with the letter, and you will have "ghunnah" 
(the exhalation of air) for 1 second  ^apEqVUcf

EXCEPTIONS TO THESE RULES: ^95H96d9r

1. There is no Merged noon when the noon is at the middle of a word  ^7EOc8FPj

2. When there is a shaddah on a noon, then you will extend for 1 sec ^Ys1Y2ypf

[[Flipped Noon]] ^oN6ZdkP7

A flipped noon happens when a noon is proceeded by a '     '.
Then the sound will change into '   ' ^8KwJypUQ

This is a very easy skill as when this happens there is a 
dedicated symbol to it ^sVMnnEVo

When this happens you have to extend ghunnah for 1 sec ^vs8FWCfh

purple ^mcEt2jUz

[[Hiding Noon]] ^CBP9OXSR

If a noon is proceeded by one of the letters that we have not talked about,
then we will make our body as if we are PREPARING to say the proceeding 
letter (but we don't say it). We slightly pronounced the noon and we have a
ghunnah of 1 second. ^VBTybYH8

mouth is positioned in a way that makes
it seem likes it preparing to say 'kha' ^OtCGKPkd
